<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="English">English</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=testing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: English">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=testing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/ˈtɛstɪŋ/</span></li>
<li>Rhymes: <a href="/wiki/Rhymes:English/%C9%9Bst%C9%AA%C5%8B" title="Rhymes:English/ɛstɪŋ"><span class="IPA">-ɛstɪŋ</span></a></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=testing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Adjective">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">testing</strong> (<i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#comparable" title="Appendix:Glossary">comparative</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/more#English" title="more">more</a> testing</b>, <i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#comparable" title="Appendix:Glossary">superlative</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/most#English" title="most">most</a> testing</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href="/wiki/difficult" title="difficult">difficult</a>, <a href="/wiki/tough" title="tough">tough</a>
<span class="HQToggle"><a>quotations ▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2011</b> June 4,  Phil McNulty,  “England 2 - 2 Switzerland”, in  <cite>BBC</cite>‎<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/sport2/hi/football/13553428.stm">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">England have now gone four games without a win at Wembley, their longest sequence without a victory in 30 years, and still have much work to do to reach Euro 2012 as they prepare for a <b>testing</b> trip to face Bulgaria in Sofia in September.</span> </div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=testing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">testing</strong> (<i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#countable" title="Appendix:Glossary">countable</a> and <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/testings#English" title="testings">testings</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The act of conducting a <a href="/wiki/test" title="test">test</a>; <a href="/wiki/trialing" title="trialing">trialing</a>, <a href="/wiki/proving" title="proving">proving</a>.
<span class="HQToggle"><a>quotations ▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><b>2011</b>, Emerson B. Powery, <i>Immersion Bible Studies: Luke</i>
<dl><dd>The wilderness <b>testings</b> of Jesus prepare him for ministry in which such temptations and shortcuts will recur.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
